     527                 :            :          * invalid PE# for the corresponding RID.

     529                 :            :          * Note: Instead we set all RTE entries to 0x00 to
     530                 :            :          * work around a problem where PE lookups might be
     531                 :            :          * done before Linux has established valid PE's
     532                 :            :          * (during PCI probing). We can revisit that once/if
     533                 :            :          * Linux has been fixed to always setup valid PEs.
     534                 :            :          *
     535                 :            :          * The value 0x00 corresponds to the default PE# Linux
     536                 :            :          * uses to check for config space freezes before it
     537                 :            :          * has assigned PE# to busses.
     538                 :            :          *
     539                 :            :          * WARNING: Additionally, we need to be careful, there's
     540                 :            :          * a HW issue, if we get an MSI on an RTT entry that is
     541                 :            :          * FF, things will go bad. We need to ensure we don't
     542                 :            :          * ever let a live FF RTT even temporarily when resetting

    3513                 :          4 : static bool phb3_wait_dlp_reset(struct phb3 *p)
    3514                 :            : {
    3515                 :            :         unsigned int i;
    3516                 :            :         uint64_t val;
    3517                 :            : 
    3518                 :            :         /*
    3519                 :            :          * Firmware cannot access the UTL core regs or PCI config space
    3520                 :            :          * until the cores are out of DL_PGRESET.
    3521                 :            :          * DL_PGRESET should be polled until it is inactive with a value
    3522                 :            :          * of '0'. The recommended polling frequency is once every 1ms.
    3523                 :            :          * Firmware should poll at least 200 attempts before giving up.
    3524                 :            :          * MMIO Stores to the link are silently dropped by the UTL core if
    3525                 :            :          * the link is down.
    3526                 :            :          * MMIO Loads to the link will be dropped by the UTL core and will
    3527                 :            :          * eventually time-out and will return an all ones response if the
    3528                 :            :          * link is down.
    3529                 :            :          */
    3530                 :            : #define DLP_RESET_ATTEMPTS      40000
    3531                 :            : 
    3532                 :          4 :         PHBDBG(p, "Waiting for DLP PG reset to complete...\n");
    3533         [ +  - ]:        498 :         for (i = 0; i < DLP_RESET_ATTEMPTS; i++) {
    3534                 :        996 :                 val = in_be64(p->regs + PHB_PCIE_DLP_TRAIN_CTL);
    3535         [ +  + ]:        498 :                 if (!(val & PHB_PCIE_DLP_TC_DL_PGRESET))
    3536                 :            :                         break;
    3537                 :        494 :                 time_wait_us(10);
    3538                 :            :         }
    3539         [ -  + ]:          4 :         if (val & PHB_PCIE_DLP_TC_DL_PGRESET) {
    3540                 :          0 :                 PHBERR(p, "Timeout waiting for DLP PG reset !\n");
    3541                 :          0 :                 return false;
    3542                 :            :         }
    3543                 :            :         return true;
    3544                 :            : }
